    unset vdom
end

config ips sensor
    edit "g-default"
        set comment "Prevent critical attacks."
        set block-malicious-url disable
        set extended-log disable
        config entries
            edit 1
                set location all
                set severity medium high critical 
                set protocol all
                set os all
                set application all
                set status default
                set log enable
                set log-packet disable
                set log-attack-context disable
                set action default
                set quarantine none
            next
        end
    next
    edit "g-sniffer-profile"
        set comment "Monitor IPS attacks."
        set block-malicious-url disable
        set extended-log disable
        config entries
            edit 1
                set location all
                set severity medium high critical 
                set protocol all
                set os all
                set application all
                set status default
                set log enable
                set log-packet disable
                set log-attack-context disable
                set action default
                set quarantine none
            next
        end
    next
    edit "g-wifi-default"
        set comment "Default configuration for offloading WiFi traffic."
        set block-malicious-url disable
        set extended-log disable
        config entries
            edit 1
                set location all
                set severity medium high critical 
                set protocol all
                set os all
                set application all
                set status default
                set log enable
                set log-packet disable
                set log-attack-context disable
                set action default
                set quarantine none
            next
        end
    next
end
  config application list
    edit "g-default"
        set comment "Monitor all applications."
        set extended-log disable
        set other-application-action pass
        set app-replacemsg enable
        set other-application-log disable
        set unknown-application-action pass
        set unknown-application-log disable
